UKR_dualism_category = {
	UKR_hetman_makes_his_move = {
		icon = GFX_decision_shield
		
		allowed = { always = no } #manually activated
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = UKR_Prepare_The_Anti_Hetman_Coup
		}
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = UKR_Prepare_The_Anti_Hetman_Coup
		}
		
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 35
		
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_hetman_makes_his_move"
			UKR_decrease_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_hetman_makes_his_move"
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_With_UVO }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1
					country_event = ukrpol.301
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2
					country_event = ukrpol.17
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3
					country_event = ukrpol.27
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_4 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_4
					country_event = ukrpol.28
				}
				else = {
					UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
					UKR_increase_hetman = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_Of_Monarchists }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1
					country_event = ukrpol.29
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2
					country_event = ukrpol.30
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3
					country_event = ukrpol.19
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = {
							id = ukrpol.20
							days = 15
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
					UKR_increase_hetman = yes
				}
			}
			activate_mission = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move
		}
	}

			}
		}
	}

political_actions = {
	UKR_recruit_teroborona = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military

		allowed = { tag = UKR }
		
		available = {
			has_war_support > 0			
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_teroborona_is_recruiting
			}
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { FROM = { has_state_flag = UKR_teroborona_recruited_@ROOT } }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 499 }
			command_power > 4
		}
		custom_cost_text = 500_infantry_equipment_1_cp_5
		days_remove = 15
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		on_map_mode = map_only

		state_target = yes
		target_array = UKR.owned_states
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		target_root_trigger = {
			has_idea = UKR_teroborona_idea
			has_defensive_war = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancel UKR_recruit_teroborona target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = 5
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 500
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_recruit_teroborona target: [From.GetName]"
			set_country_flag = UKR_teroborona_is_recruiting
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -5
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -500
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove UKR_recruit_teroborona target: [From.GetName]"
			clr_country_flag = UKR_teroborona_is_recruiting
			FROM = {
				set_state_flag = UKR_teroborona_recruited_@ROOT
				### calculate number of units to spawn
				set_temp_variable = { units_to_spawn = state_population_k }
				divide_temp_variable = { units_to_spawn = 500 }

				### failsafe so at least one unit is always spawned
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = units_to_spawn min = 1 max = 7 }

				### tooltip
				set_temp_variable = { total_units_to_spawn = units_to_spawn }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_recruit_teroborona_units

				### spawn normal militias
				set_temp_variable = { counter = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { var = units_to_spawn value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					}
					ROOT = { 
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_template = "Teroborona" }
							}
							division_template = {
								name = "Teroborona"
								division_names_group = UKR_MIL_01
								regiments = {
									militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
									militia = { x = 2 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
								}
								support = {
									recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									military_police = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								}
								priority = 0
							}
						}
					}
					for_loop_effect = {
						start = 1
						end = units_to_spawn
						compare = less_than_or_equals

						meta_effect = {
							text = {
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = [DIVISION] division_template = \"Teroborona\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 1"
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
									owner = ROOT
								}
							}
							DIVISION = "\\\"[?counter]a [THIS.GetName] Okrema Bryhada Teritorialnoi Oborony\\\""
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { counter = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

					division = "division_template = \"Interbrigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.8"
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}

	KCN_vote_timer = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse
		allowed = { always = no } #manually activated
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 30
		is_good = no

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout KCN_vote_timer"
			clr_global_flag = KCN_vote_ongoing
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_cultural_research_cooperation_vote }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_cultural_research_cooperation_vote
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.72 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_economic_cooperation_vote }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_economic_cooperation_vote
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.69 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_vote }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_vote
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.79 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_revoke }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_revoke
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.87 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes }
					}
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.68 hours = 2 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.67 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
			clear_variable = global.kcn_yes_votes
			clear_variable = global.kcn_no_votes
			clear_variable = global.kcn_abstain_votes
		}
	}
}

					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_chernihiv
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_poltava
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_kharkiv
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_katerinoslav
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_crimea
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_kherson
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_podillia
					NOT = { has_country_flag = king_has_visited_volyn }
					OR = {
						NOT = { owns_state = 91 }
						has_country_flag = king_has_visited_galicia
					}
				}
				country_event = ukrmisc.28 #King visits Volyn
			}			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_kyiv
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_chernihiv
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_poltava
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_kharkiv
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_katerinoslav
					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_crimea

					has_country_flag = king_has_visited_volyn
					OR = {
						NOT = { owns_state = 91 }
						has_country_flag = king_has_visited_galicia
					}
				}
				country_event = ukrmisc.37 #Royal Tour Ends
			}			
		}

							check_variable = { UKR_second_ingridient = 4 }

					}

							check_variable = { UKR_second_ingridient = 8 }

					}

			add_stability = 0.05
			increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_Agricultural_Crisis_deadline"
			add_stability = 0.05
			increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_Agricultural_Crisis_deadline"
			decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_30 = yes
			add_stability = -0.3
		}
